<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal 2023 Third-quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>and Raises Full-year Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

20&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of $0.92 was down 15&nbsp;percent from the prior year; adjusted diluted EPS
of $0.97 was up 17&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company raises full-year fiscal 2023 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 8 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (Mar. 23, 2023) &#150;
General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for its fiscal 2023 third quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We built on our positive momentum and
delivered strong results in the third quarter, including broad-based growth across each of our segments,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Our team continues to manage well through ongoing supply
chain disruptions and volatility in the operating environment. Our brands are winning with consumers, and we plan to sustain this momentum by continuing to invest in brand building, innovation, and capabilities that will drive future growth. With
strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-date</FONT></FONT> performance and good visibility to the fourth quarter, we are once again raising our fiscal 2023 outlook for our key financial measures.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and standing
for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to further
enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Third Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 13&nbsp;percent to $5.1&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 16&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, with organic pound volume essentially matching <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 160 basis points to 32.5&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects. Adjusted gross margin was up 240 basis points to 33.8&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation and higher other cost of goods sold. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $730&nbsp;million was down 10&nbsp;percent, reflecting higher selling, general, and
administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses and a lower net gain on divestitures, partially offset by higher gross profit dollars. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 14.2&nbsp;percent was down 380 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit
increased 20&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment. Adjusted operating profit margin increased 80 basis points to
15.7&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> declined 16&nbsp;percent to $553&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was down 15&nbsp;percent to $0.92, driven by lower operating profit, lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures, higher net interest expense, and lower benefit plan
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income, partially offset by lower net shares outstanding. Adjusted diluted EPS of $0.97 increased 17&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher adjusted operating profit and lower net
shares outstanding, partially offset by lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures, higher net interest expense, a higher adjusted effective tax rate, and lower benefit plan
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Nine Month Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 7&nbsp;percent to $15.1&nbsp;billion, including a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> headwind from net divestiture and acquisition activity and 1 point of unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales increased 12&nbsp;percent, driven by positive organic net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 80 basis points to 32.0&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs,
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, and the impact of market index pricing on bakery flour, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross
margin was up 110 basis points to 33.9&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and the impact of market index pricing on bakery flour. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $2.6&nbsp;billion was up 6&nbsp;percent, driven by net gains on divestitures and
higher gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher SG&amp;A expenses and unfavorable net corporate investment activity.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 17.4&nbsp;percent essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
levels. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit increased 11&nbsp;percent, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment. Adjusted
operating profit margin increased 60 basis points to 17.0&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> increased 5&nbsp;percent to $2.0&nbsp;billion and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 7&nbsp;percent to $3.28, primarily reflecting higher operating profit and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures and lower benefit plan <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. Adjusted diluted EPS of $3.18 was up 14&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, a lower adjusted effective tax rate, and lower net shares
outstanding, partially offset by lower <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures and lower benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Notes on Comparability </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Financial results in the first
nine months of fiscal 2023 reflected the acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treat business in the first quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of the European yogurt business in the third quarter of fiscal 2022; the divestiture of certain
international dough businesses in the third and fourth quarters of fiscal 2022; the acquisition of the TNT Crust foodservice business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023; and the divestiture of the Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes
business in the first quarter of fiscal 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Nine-month results in fiscal 2023 also included the impact of a voluntary recall on certain
international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products, which was a headwind to net sales and operating profit results in the International segment. Unallocated corporate items in the first nine months
included an additional $26&nbsp;million of charges related to product disposals associated with the ice cream recall that were excluded from adjusted operating profit results. The company does not expect a further material impact from the ice cream
recall going forward. </P>
</DIV></Center>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 15&nbsp;percent to $3.2&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> headwind from divestitures and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from unfavorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales
increased 18&nbsp;percent. Net sales increased 22&nbsp;percent in U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions, 19&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks, and 7&nbsp;percent in U.S. Morning Foods. Constant-currency net sales were up 8&nbsp;percent in Canada. Segment
operating profit of $787&nbsp;million was up 29&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses, including a
double-digit increase in media investment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America Retail segment net sales increased 12&nbsp;percent to
$9.6&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-point</FONT> headwind from divestitures. Organic net sales were up 14&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $2.4&nbsp;billion was up 24&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant
currency, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs, lower volume, and higher SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the Pet segment
increased 14&nbsp;percent to $646&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and increased pound volume. Organic net sales were also up 14&nbsp;percent. Net sales performance represented an acceleration from second quarter
results, driven by improved customer service, increased brand-building and other commercial activities, and a rebuild of retailer inventory. Segment operating profit of $103&nbsp;million was down 7&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by input cost
inflation, increased costs related to capacity expansion and service improvement, and higher SG&amp;A expenses, including a double-digit increase in media investment, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix, HMM cost savings, and
higher volume. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, Pet segment net sales increased 10&nbsp;percent to $1.8&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats acquisition. Organic net sales were up 9&nbsp;percent. Retailer inventory was stable in the first nine months, with estimated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-channel</FONT>
retail sales up high-single digits. Segment operating profit was down 13&nbsp;percent to $312&nbsp;million, driven primarily by higher input costs, higher SG&amp;A expenses, and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net price realization and
mix. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 25&nbsp;percent to $548&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price
realization and mix, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> benefit from market index pricing on bakery flour. Net sales results also included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust
acquisition. Organic net sales were up 19&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 134&nbsp;percent to $82&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix, partially offset by higher input costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America Foodservice net sales increased 23&nbsp;percent to $1.6&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> benefit from the TNT Crust acquisition. Organic net sales were up 18&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 24&nbsp;percent to $218&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization
and mix, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the International segment were down 3&nbsp;percent to $701&nbsp;million, driven by lower pound volume, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> headwind from divestitures, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were
up 8&nbsp;percent, with broad-based growth across Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia, distributor markets, Brazil, and China. Segment operating profit of $42&nbsp;million was up 18&nbsp;percent as reported and up 27&nbsp;percent in constant currency,
driven by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by higher input costs and lower volume, including the impact of divestitures. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, International net sales were down 21&nbsp;percent to $2.0&nbsp;billion,
driven by lower pound volume, largely reflecting the impact of the yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5-point</FONT> headwind from foreign currency exchange, partially offset by favorable
net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up 3&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $95&nbsp;million was down 39&nbsp;percent as reported and down 33&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by lower volume, including the impacts
of the yogurt and dough divestitures and the ice cream recall, and higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter
constant-currency net sales increased 2&nbsp;percent for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) and were up 1&nbsp;percent for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ). Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT>
earnings from joint ventures totaled $13&nbsp;million compared to $30&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by higher input costs and unfavorable nonrecurring discrete tax items at CPW, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix
at CPW. Through nine months, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures totaled $58&nbsp;million compared to $92&nbsp;million a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated
corporate items totaled $296&nbsp;million net expense in the third quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to $141&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT>
valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $206&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to $117&nbsp;million net expense last year, driven primarily by higher compensation and benefits expense,
corporate charitable contributions, and capability investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $1&nbsp;million
in the third quarter of fiscal 2023 compared to $7&nbsp;million a year ago <I>(please see Note 4 below for more information on these charges)</I>. Benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income totaled $22&nbsp;million in
the third quarter compared to $27&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by an increase in interest cost, partially offset by lower amortization of losses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense of $98&nbsp;million was up 14&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by higher interest rates, partially offset by lower average
long-term debt balances. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 16.6&nbsp;percent compared to 16.3&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 7 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was
21.6&nbsp;percent compared to 21.0&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $2.0&nbsp;billion through nine months of fiscal 2023 compared to $2.2&nbsp;billion a year ago, driven primarily
by an increase in inventory and higher cash tax payments. Capital investments of $351&nbsp;million essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels. Dividends paid increased 4&nbsp;percent to $967&nbsp;million. General
Mills repurchased approximately 15&nbsp;million shares of common stock through nine months of fiscal 2023 for a total of $1.2&nbsp;billion compared to $550&nbsp;million in share repurchases a year ago. Average diluted shares outstanding through nine
months decreased 2&nbsp;percent to 602&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2023 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills continues to expect the largest factors impacting its performance in fiscal 2023 will be the economic health of consumers, the inflationary cost
environment, and the frequency and severity of disruptions in the supply chain. For the full year, the company continues to expect input cost inflation of 14 to 15&nbsp;percent of total cost of goods sold, HMM cost savings of 3 to 4&nbsp;percent of
cost of goods sold, moderately lower supply chain disruptions compared to the prior year, and increased investment in brand building and other growth-driving activities. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With stronger and more broad-based business momentum, the company is raising its outlook for fiscal 2023.
The updated full-year financial targets are summarized below&sup1;: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

of approximately 10&nbsp;percent growth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed a new organization structure to streamline our global
operations. This global reorganization required us to reevaluate our operating segments. Under our new organization structure, our chief operating decision maker assesses performance and makes decisions about resources to be allocated to our
operating segments as follows: North America Retail; International; Pet; and North America Foodservice. We have restated our net sales by segment and segment operating profit amounts to reflect our new operating segments. These segment changes had
no effect on previously reported consolidated net sales, operating profit, net earnings attributable to General Mills, or earnings per share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we acquired TNT Crust, a manufacturer of high-quality frozen pizza
crusts for regional and national pizza chains, foodservice distributors, and retail outlets, for a purchase price of $253&nbsp;million. We financed the transaction with U.S. commercial paper. We consolidated the TNT Crust business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $154&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the North America Foodservice segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. The
consolidated results of the TNT Crust business are reported in our North America Foodservice segment on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2023, we completed the asset sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business to Eagle
Family Foods Group for $607&nbsp;million and recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $442&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for Sodiaal&#146;s interest in our Canadian yogurt
business, a modified agreement for the use of <I>Yoplait</I> and <I>Libert&eacute;</I> brands in the United States and Canada, and cash. We recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $150&nbsp;million on the sale of these
businesses during the third quarter of fiscal 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we sold a European dough business and
recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain on sale of $21&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of fiscal 2022,
we acquired Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated the pet treats business into our Consolidated Balance Sheets and
recorded goodwill of $762&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I>, and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer relationship asset of
$40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet segment and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, we did not undertake any new restructuring actions. We
recorded $2&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the third quarter of fiscal 2023 and $16&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, related to restructuring actions previously announced. We
recorded $9&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the third quarter of fiscal 2022 and $8&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, related to restructuring actions previously announced. We
expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2024. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $296&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to
$141&nbsp;million in the same period in fiscal 2022. In the third quarter of fiscal 2023, we recorded a $67&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the

interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses. In addition, certain compensation and benefits expenses and charitable contributions increased in the third quarter
of fiscal 2023, compared to the same period last year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $842&nbsp;million in the

decrease in expense in the same period last year. We recorded $82&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments and the sale of corporate investments in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, compared to $21&nbsp;million
of net gains in the same period last year. In the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, we recorded a $26&nbsp;million charge related to a voluntary recall on certain international
<I>H</I><I>&auml;</I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice cream products. In addition, we recorded $5&nbsp;million of integration costs primarily related to our acquisition of TNT Crust in the nine-month period ended
February&nbsp;26, 2023, compared to $20&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. In the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26,
2023, we recorded $2&nbsp;million of transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business compared to $57&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait
SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses. In addition, we recorded a $20&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item and a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery in the
nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. In addition, certain compensation and benefits expenses and charitable contributions increased in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, compared to the same period last year. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the third quarter of fiscal 2023 was 16.6&nbsp;percent compared to 16.3&nbsp;percent
for the third quarter of fiscal 2022. The 0.3 percentage point increase was primarily due to certain unfavorable nonrecurring discrete tax items, partially offset by favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2023. Our effective tax
rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 21.6&nbsp;percent in the third quarter of fiscal 2023, compared to 21.0&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148;
section below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.6 percentage point increase was primarily due to certain unfavorable nonrecurring discrete tax items, partially offset by favorable changes in earnings mix by
jurisdiction in the third quarter of fiscal 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for the nine-month period ended
February&nbsp;26, 2023, was 19.6&nbsp;percent compared to 19.9&nbsp;percent in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. The 0.3 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits and favorable
changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction, partially offset by certain unfavorable tax components related to the divestitures incurred in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting
comparability was 20.8&nbsp;percent in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;26, 2023, compared to 21.7&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; section below for a
description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.9 percentage point decrease is primarily due to certain nonrecurring discrete tax benefits and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in the nine-month period ended
February&nbsp;26, 2023. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(8)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors, and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our
consolidated net sales and segment net sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes.
We believe that organic net sales growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations,
acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales
growth rates, the relevant GAAP measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are
presented excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at
the average exchange rates in effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year
results in local currencies multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide
useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2023 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow
conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions,
divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without
unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2023. The unavailable
information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2023 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2023, we currently expect: foreign
currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and completed acquisitions and divestitures to reduce net sales growth by approximately 4.5&nbsp;percent; foreign currency exchange rates to reduce
adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth by approximately 1&nbsp;percent; and restructuring charges and project-related costs, transaction and acquisition integration costs related to actions previously announced, and product
disposal charges related to the ice cream recall to total approximately $55&nbsp;million to $60&nbsp;million. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net divestitures gain primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023.
Divestitures gain related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of a European dough business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2023. Valuation adjustments and the gain on sale of
certain corporate investments in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Voluntary recall costs recorded in fiscal 2023 related to certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I>
ice cream products. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions recorded in fiscal 2023 and fiscal 2022. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs primarily resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust in fiscal 2023. Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of
Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs primarily related to the sale of our Helper main meals and Suddenly Salad side dishes business in fiscal 2023. Transaction
costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and the sale of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax recovery </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth on a Constant-currency Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted operating
profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Diluted EPS and Related Constant-currency Growth Rates </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors
because it is the profitability measure we use to evaluate earnings performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Constant-currency Segment Operating Profit Growth Rates </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to underlying performance of our segments by excluding
the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our segments&#146; operating profit growth rates on a constant-currency basis are calculated as follows: </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Net Sales Growth Rates for Our Canada Operating Unit on a Constant-currency Basis</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure of our Canada operating unit net sales provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to underlying
performance of our Canada operating unit within our North America Retail segment by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
